// ============================================= // v4.2 - Mobile Filter Bottom Sheet Logic // ============================================= (function() { const fab = document.getElementById('mobileFilterFab'); const overlay = document.getElementById('mobileFilterOverlay'); const sheet = document.getElementById('mobileFilterSheet'); const closeBtn = document.getElementById('mobileFilterClose'); const badge = document.getElementById('filterBadge'); const mobileSearch = document.getElementById('mobileSearchInput'); const mobilePriority = document.getElementById('mobilePriorityFilter'); const mobileOwner = document.getElementById('mobileOwnerFilter'); const mobileSort = document.getElementById('mobileSortSelect'); const mobileReset = document.getElementById('mobileResetFilters'); const mobileLabelFilters = document.getElementById('mobileLabelFilters'); // Desktop counterparts const desktopSearch = document.getElementById('searchInput'); const desktopPriority = document.getElementById('priorityFilter'); const desktopOwner = document.getElementById('ownerFilter'); const desktopSort = document.getElementById('sortSelect'); const desktopLabelFilters = document.getElementById('labelFilters'); if (!fab || !sheet) return; function openSheet() { overlay.style.display = 'block'; sheet.style.display = 'block'; requestAnimationFrame(() => { overlay.classList.add('visible'); sheet.classList.add('open'); }); document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden'; // Sync current filter state from desktop controls if (desktopSearch) mobileSearch.value = desktopSearch.value; if (desktopPriority) mobilePriority.value = desktopPriority.value; if (desktopOwner) mobileOwner.value = desktopOwner.value; if (desktopSort) mobileSort.value = desktopSort.value; syncLabelPills(); } function closeSheet() { overlay.classList.remove('visible'); sheet.classList.remove('open'); document.body.style.overflow = ''; setTimeout(() => { overlay.style.display = 'none'; sheet.style.display = 'none'; }, 300); } function syncLabelPills() { if (!desktopLabelFilters || !mobileLabelFilters) return; mobileLabelFilters.innerHTML = desktopLabelFilters.innerHTML; // Re-bind click events on the cloned pills mobileLabelFilters.querySelectorAll('.label-pill').forEach(pill => { pill.addEventListener('click', () => { const label = pill.dataset.label; // Find and click the matching desktop pill const desktopPill = desktopLabelFilters.querySelector('[data-label="' + label + '"]'); if (desktopPill) desktopPill.click(); // Sync active states after a tick setTimeout(syncLabelPills, 50); updateBadge(); }); }); } function applyFilter(mobileEl, desktopEl) { if (!desktopEl) return; desktopEl.value = mobileEl.value; desktopEl.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles: true})); updateBadge(); } function updateBadge() { let count = 0; if (desktopSearch && desktopSearch.value) count++; if (desktopPriority && desktopPriority.value) count++; if (desktopOwner && desktopOwner.value) count++; if (desktopLabelFilters) { const activePills = desktopLabelFilters.querySelectorAll('.label-pill.active'); count += activePills.length; } badge.textContent = count > 0 ? count : ''; } fab.addEventListener('click', openSheet); overlay.addEventListener('click', closeSheet); closeBtn.addEventListener('click', closeSheet); mobileSearch.addEventListener('input', () => { if (desktopSearch) { desktopSearch.value = mobileSearch.value; desktopSearch.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', {bubbles: true})); } updateBadge(); }); mobilePriority.addEventListener('change', () => applyFilter(mobilePriority, desktopPriority)); mobileOwner.addEventListener('change', () => applyFilter(mobileOwner, desktopOwner)); mobileSort.addEventListener('change', () => applyFilter(mobileSort, desktopSort)); mobileReset.addEventListener('click', () => { mobileSearch.value = ''; mobilePriority.value = ''; mobileOwner.value = ''; mobileSort.value = 'date'; if (desktopSearch) { desktopSearch.value = ''; desktopSearch.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', {bubbles: true})); } if (desktopPriority) { desktopPriority.value = ''; desktopPriority.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles: true})); } if (desktopOwner) { desktopOwner.value = ''; desktopOwner.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles: true})); } if (desktopSort) { desktopSort.value = 'date'; desktopSort.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles: true})); } // Reset label pills if (desktopLabelFilters) { desktopLabelFilters.querySelectorAll('.label-pill.active').forEach(p => p.click()); } setTimeout(() => { syncLabelPills(); updateBadge(); }, 100); }); // Update badge on page load and whenever filters change const observer = new MutationObserver(() => { updateBadge(); }); if (desktopLabelFilters) observer.observe(desktopLabelFilters, {childList: true, subtree: true, attributes: true}); setTimeout(updateBadge, 1000); // Swipe-down to close the sheet let touchStartY = 0; sheet.addEventListener('touchstart', (e) => { touchStartY = e.touches[0].clientY; }, {passive: true}); sheet.addEventListener('touchmove', (e) => { const dy = e.touches[0].clientY - touchStartY; if (dy > 80 && sheet.scrollTop <= 0) closeSheet(); }, {passive: true}); })();
